< username>
Jon V.</username>
<Pictures>None<//Pictures><Resp>None<//Resp>< Text>
Reviewed on 2018-11-09

We have been to this place several times and mostly when the kids invite us to go.  My children enjoy the outside seating; a perfect place to hang out, especially during summer.

The self-serve dispensers come with loads of yogurt flavors. There are mini sample cups readily available to try each tang.

For consumer seeking seasonal limited-time flavor like myself, the factory has the pumpkin froyo.  We love the seasonal flavors as they trigger excitement, which in this case, make us look forward to the Thanksgiving and Christmas Holidays.

There are a variety of toppings to choose that spurs creativity. I always get the cheesecake in cubes, which is constantly stored in the fridge to keep it fresh.  A scoop of garden-fresh blueberries and coconut jelly to add makes the dessert healthy and enjoyable to eat.

Then, there are the spoons that change color as it reacts to cold yogurt temperatures continue to keep us entertained.

The staff members here are personable and never fail to greet each time we visit.   The place and the bathroom are clean, which speaks a lot about the establishment.

Not only is the pricing is fairly reasonable, the froyo parlor also offers 25% discount to Yelper users (a plus) and 10% discount to firefighters and military service members.

This is by far the best yogurt chain in the Temecula area.<//Text>

< text>
The very best yogurt - quality, variety, flavors.  Hands down!

Yogurt Factory always has the best yogurts in town.  A great variety of flavors and toppings, and at least one low-carb flavor.
The are very generous, too.  They use a punch card/frequent buyer system, along with the SpotOn application, so its easy to earn free yogurt.  They also offer coupons for email and Instagram customers.  They offer a great value for the money.  Favorite flavors are Pistachio Pudding and Creamy Coconut, but they are all delicious!

I feel like I'm giving away a great secret, but Yogurt Factory really is the best frozen yogurt in the valley!< /text>

< text>
I do not know if they were trying to be ironic, but this is not a "coin less" laundromat. There are machines to get change in quarters. If you think you can be productive on your laptop or stream on your phone, this particular location did not let me use my Verizon network, nor my backup Visible phone reliably. While this is not their fault, it's just a heads up to anyone with that in mind. They have small and large washers where you can try to limit the number of loads you may have to wash, but at $3 and $5.50 respectively, I would say this is pretty expensive. It would be nice if they provided wifi access as a perk. Otherwise the machines still look new, but I may be looking to try other laundromats. Also last wash is at 8:30, which feels a little early although they close at 10pm.< /text>

< review>
I have heard mixed Customer Service reviews about this location from members of my Firm, along with some from family and friends, so I decided to investigate for myself. Today I ordered an online Special that included Cheese Sticks. I specifically requested that the Garlic Sauce come with the sticks, instead of the default pizza sauce. When I received the order there was pizza sauce in the box, although my receipt and the order sticker attached to the box clearly stated Garlic Sauce. When I showed the "large, heavy-set" elderly fellow--clearly one of the pizza makers, based on his attire--the box label and pizza sauce he replied "Oh, you want something else?!" I told him I just wanted what I ordered. So the now clearly disturbed pizza maker grabs a garlic sauce container from under the counter, and without making eye contact chucks the container in my direction. When I thank him, he ignores me and walks away. So I say "it's 'You're welcome', Sir.", he tells me "You're done. Goodbye". I guess the Garlic Sauce was coming out of his check or something! To add insult to injury, the "All the Meats" pizza I ordered had not one sliver of pepperoni or bacon on it--just sausage, ham and cheese! In any event, it would seem the rumors were true. My firm will be cutting off any continued donations to any Papa John's programs and this location will be recognized via letter sent Papa's Corporate Leadership. The 'customer' only asked for what was ordered, guys. It's only a sauce container, yet the 'employee' made it into an issue. Missing toppings is unacceptable, especially when there is a chart regarding which toppings go on Specialties posted above your pizza prep station.</review>

The best part is that they inquired about my shipping quotes, which were $90 UPS, and $75 USPS. They mentioned that they shipped UPS, and would like to see if they could beat my quotes. I laughed thinking that I already had a UPS quote, what was the point? They measured and weighed the box, added the appropriate insurance on it, and beat not only my UPS quote, but also the USPS one too! $63 bucks!!!!!! That was a huge drop, and I was extremely thankful for it! It's customer service like this that I wish was everywhere. The sad thing is that it's really rare to be treated like a valued customer with important business. The UPS store and my local USPS didn't give me confidence that my package was important and delicate, or that it would arrive in one piece. Missouri Flat Storage did.  Ralph must have put a pound of tape on the outside of the box (which was already used once and had some dings in it) to reinforce cardboard and it's rigidity.  Neither of them tried to up sell me on packing products... even went looking for some that might have been left over from others! I swear I will never taking my moving, storing, and now shipping business anywhere else. The food here is good and it's nice to eat at a family owned restaurant. Location is nice, small and casual. Nice drink and food selection. Great sides as well as quality bagels and other breads. < review>
This is a very good fast casual Mexican place for breakfast lunch dinner in Mountain View.  The Mountain View special burrito is my favorite its tasty fresh juicy rich and decent price. They have good tacos and a breakfast menu. Plus good Mexican refreshment drinks like Horchata and Rose drink. You will pay few bucks more on average than Taco Bell but you will get consistently better Mexican food. In the COVID time they are operating solid take out service with quick order completion. It's been a Best of Mountain View award winner for many years! Its kind of a hidden gem in a small strip mall.< /review>

< Text>
I'm lucky to have moved in right around the corner from the area's best burrito place! I recommend the Pollo en mole. They stew it fresh every day. One day I arrived right when they opened, and they had to ask back to the guy stirring this huge pot if it was ready yet. You may have to wait until it's properly lunch time for this treat!

La Coste√±a has been a great resource when we invite a number of friends over for a game day. We can all walk down there and everyone can have a nice custom made meal.

A lot of people get takeout here, and they keep the line moving quickly. If you want to sit (indoors, outdoors, or at their large community table), there is always plenty of room.

They are generous with their portions. They are precise with making everything as ordered.

They have vegetarian and vegan options. Ask them to customize any way you need. Since they make everything fresh they are knowledgeable about all the ingredients. It may not be a good pick, though, for those with highly sensitive allergies, as they can't guarantee there won't be cross-contamination from the assembly-line style of preparation.< /Text>

This was the first e-commerce site, when Sun engineers set up a fax+ xwindows tool(xburrito) to order from your desktop in the early 1980s. It was a grocery store then where you could order your custom burrito by pointing to what you wanted. Then Run by an old husband and wife team. Now the store has moved to a new location, and the ordering process has changed. The burrito is still good, but you can no longer ask for exactly what you want. The large one can still feed a family of four. Still one of the better burrito in town< /Text>

This was the first e-commerce site, when Sun engineers set up a fax+ xwindows tool(xburrito) to order from your desktop in the early 1980s. It was a grocery store then where you could order your custom burrito by pointing to what you wanted. Then Run by an old husband and wife team. Now the store has moved to a new location, and the ordering process has changed. The burrito is still good, but you can no longer ask for exactly what you want. The large one can still feed a family of four. Still one of the better burrito in town<//text>

< Review>
SUPER BURRITO????? I have been to many different places where they have a "super burrito" and from what I've notice is that it's called "super" because they add more "prime" ingredients not just for the size. I order a so called " super burrito" and for the $13 I paid I was expecting much more then what I got. And what I got is not even worth $5. My "super burrito" had beans, rice, salsa Verde, and just SOME carne asada, and I said some because it was only like a soup spoon of meat in the middle. Very disappointed. Not worth the money I spent.<//Review>

101243954824006425652<//user_id>
<Resp>None< /Resp><Review>Best burritos in Mountain View hands down. Cheap also!< /Review></record></dataset><record>
<Review>[From August 2008]

I ordered an enchilada platter today and was pretty darn pleased.

PORTION: Large, but not humongous.  That's fine :)
BEANS (whole): Cooked nicely, decent scoop, a bit watery, though (lady was too impatient to let it drain).
SALSA (mild): Don't really taste it in the mix.  To their credit, they have a selection of salsas.
GUAC: Really tasty!  Seems decently fresh.
MEAT (chicken mole):  Cooked perfectly (tender, not dry).  Nicely seasoned, but nothing amazing.
ENCHILADA:  Grilled with cheese on it, not microwaved!  This may seem like a no-duh idea, but I've been bummed at how many Mexican places just nuke their enchiladas!
CHIPS:  None offered.  Hey, that sucks :-(
COST:  Not too bad, but charging for everything extra is annoying.
DRINK:  Maybe I missed it, but no horchata and such?  WTH?
SERVICE:  Okay.  Woman wasn't particularly friendly.
PARKING:  Yeah, it generally sucks, but there were two open spaces on this Sunday afternoon.

People rave about La Bamba compared to this?!  You can see my review of that place, but in a nutshell, why?!?  La Bamba offered practically no customization (not even choices of salsa?!?), and their burrito tasted more like a quesadilla to me... way too much cheese.  Yuck.< /Review><Response>None<//Response>< pictures>
None<//pictures>
